create_vassal_with_religion_and_culture = {
	hidden_effect = {
		$tag$ = {
			change_religion = $religion$
			remove_country_modifier = conversion_zeal
			clr_country_flag = changed_religion
			change_primary_culture = $culture$
			remove_country_modifier = restructuring_administration
		}
	}
	create_vassal = $tag$
}

release_with_religion_and_culture = {
	hidden_effect = {
		$tag$ = {
			change_religion = $religion$
			remove_country_modifier = conversion_zeal
			clr_country_flag = changed_religion
			change_primary_culture = $culture$
			remove_country_modifier = restructuring_administration
		}
	}
	release = $tag$
}

estate_action_CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS = {
	add_country_modifier = {
		name = "estate_adventurers_cavern_exploration_initiative_mod"
		duration = 3650
	}
	create_leader_scaling_with_tradition = {
		leader = conquistador
		type = army
	}
}

change_tag_and_keep_color = {
	hidden_effect = { save_event_target_as = colorswap }
	change_tag = $tag$
	custom_tooltip = change_tag_keep_color_tt
	hidden_effect = { change_country_color = { country = event_target:colorswap } }
}

cleanup_empty_province = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_empty = yes
		}
		
		province_event = {
			id = deletecolony.1
		}
	}
}

# Centaur Nomadic Zone of Control Effects

apply_owned_NZOC_country = {
	save_event_target_as = the_centaur_who_moved #Needed because ROOT is different in the 2 places this is fired
	every_owned_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control
		remove_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
		remove_province_modifier = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control
		remove_province_modifier = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
	}

	capital_scope = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = centaur } } owner = { has_country_flag = majority_setup_complete } }
			add_centaur_minority_size_effect = yes
		}
		
		hidden_effect = { add_local_autonomy = -100 }

		#GIVE MODIFIERS TO CAPITAL
		apply_all_owned_NZOC_province = yes

		#GIVE MODIFIERS TO OWNED NEIGHBORING PROVINCES
		every_neighbor_province = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = event_target:the_centaur_who_moved
				has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = no
			}
			apply_all_owned_NZOC_province = yes
		}
		
		apply_black_herd_capital_NZOC_effects = yes #Black Herd
	}

	#Golden Tremor - Permanent NZoC Province
	if = {
		limit = { has_saved_global_event_target = I57_permanent_capital_target }
		event_target:I57_permanent_capital_target = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = no }
				apply_all_owned_NZOC_province = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	apply_debuff_NZOC_country_scope = yes

	country_event = { id = centaur_nomad.200 }
}

apply_owned_centaur_NZOC_province = {
	hidden_effect = {
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { PREV = { has_province_flag = cen_double_nzoc_effects_flag } }
				add_horde_unity = 1
				change_government_reform_progress = 2
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_horde_unity
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_reform_progress
					value = 2
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_horde_unity = 0.5
				change_government_reform_progress = 1
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_horde_unity
					value = 0.5
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_reform_progress
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

apply_owned_noncentaur_NZOC_province = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = cen_double_nzoc_effects_flag }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control
				duration = -1
			}
			owner = { 
				change_government_reform_progress = 4 
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_reform_progress
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
				duration = -1
			}
			owner = { 
				change_government_reform_progress = 2 
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_reform_progress
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

apply_all_owned_NZOC_province = {

	#Add basic NZoC Modifier
	hidden_effect = { add_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes }

	#Apply effects if a centaur province
	if = {
		limit = { culture_group = centaur }
		apply_owned_centaur_NZOC_province = yes
	}

	#Otherwise apply non-centaur effects
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_gozlamoir_system }
			NOT = { culture_group = centaur }
		}
		apply_owned_noncentaur_NZOC_province = yes
	}
	
	owner = {
		#Increment variable for tooltip
		change_variable = {
			which = nzoc_provinces_affected_positive
			value = 1
		}

		if = { #Golden Tremor
			limit = { has_country_flag = I57_nzoc_effects_flag }
			add_manpower = 1 
			change_variable = {
				which = NZOC_manpower
				value = 1000
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PREV = { I57_won_negeal = yes } }
				change_government_reform_progress = 5 
				change_variable = {
					which = NZOC_reform_progress
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #Black Herd
		limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = I55_vanishing_migration } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = I55_charnelshafts
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

apply_debuff_NZOC_country_scope = {	
	capital_scope = {
		every_neighbor_province = { #add modifiers and claims to all unowned neighbor provinces
			limit = { NOT = { owned_by = event_target:the_centaur_who_moved } }

			#add normal claims
			add_claim = event_target:the_centaur_who_moved

			#add extra claims for rule from the storm
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:the_centaur_who_moved = { 
						has_government_attribute = rule_from_the_storm_effect 
					} 
				}
				every_neighbor_province = {
					add_claim = event_target:the_centaur_who_moved
				}
			}

			#increment debuffed province count
			event_target:the_centaur_who_moved = {
				change_variable = {
    				which = nzoc_provinces_affected_negative
    				value = 1
   				}
			}			
		}
	}
}

apply_pre_modifiers_NZOC_country = {
	#TIER 5 CHOICE 1 CENTAUR PATRONAGE
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = centaur_patronage_migrate_effect
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 4
				has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
				culture_is_centaur = no
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centaur_patrons_of_the_arts_pre
			duration = 7300
		}
	}

	#TIER 5 CHOICE 3. GOZLAMOIR SYSTEM EXPANSION
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = gozlamoir_expansion_migrate_effect
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 3
				has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
				culture_is_human = yes
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gozlamoir_expansion_pre
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	#TIER 5 CHOICE 2 OGRISH PRODUCTION METHODS
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = ogrish_production_migrate_effect
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 2
				has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
				OR = {
					trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
					trade_goods = gold
					trade_goods = coal
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = fires_of_industry_pre
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	#TIER 5 CHOICE 4 MODERNIZE ORDSIWYN
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = reformed_ordsiwyn_migrate_effect
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 4
				has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
				culture_is_centaur = yes
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = modernize_the_ordsiwyn_pre
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

centaur_consume_pre_modifiers_country = {
	#GOZLAMOIR
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = gozlamoir_expansion_pre }
		remove_country_modifier = gozlamoir_expansion_pre
		capital_scope = {	
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gozlamoir_expansion_post_province
				duration = 1825
			}
			every_neighbor_province = { #add modifier to OWNED neighbor provinces
				limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gozlamoir_expansion_post_province
					duration = 1825
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#OGRE
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = fires_of_industry_pre }
		remove_country_modifier = fires_of_industry_pre
		capital_scope = {
			artillery = ROOT
			owner = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = fires_of_industry_post_country
					duration = 1825
				}
			}
		}		
	}

	#TIER 5 CHOICE 1 CENTAUR PATRONAGE
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = centaur_patrons_of_the_arts_pre }
		remove_country_modifier = centaur_patrons_of_the_arts_pre
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centaur_patrons_of_the_arts_post
			duration = 7300
		}
		capital_scope = {
			add_next_institution_embracement = 15
		}
	}

	#TIER 5 CHOICE 4
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = modernize_the_ordsiwyn_pre }
		remove_country_modifier = modernize_the_ordsiwyn_pre
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = modernize_the_ordsiwyn_post
			duration = 1825
		}
	}
}

apply_reform_modifiers_NZOC_country = {
	#TIER 2 CHOICE 1. NEGEAL
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = centaur_negeal_reform_migrate_effect
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 4
				has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
				culture_is_centaur = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #Golden Tremor
			limit = { mission_completed = I57_5_3_ordsiwyn_reforms }
			add_yearly_manpower = 1.5
			capital_scope = {
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.75
			capital_scope = {
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	#TIER 2 CHOICE 2. ENSURE ORDSIWYN LOYALTIES
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = centaur_ensure_ordsiwyn_loyalties_reform_migrate_effect
			OR = {
				AND = { #Golden Tremor
					mission_completed = I57_5_3_ordsiwyn_reforms
					any_owned_province = {
						has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
						OR = {
							trade_goods = wool
							trade_goods = ivory
							trade_goods = livestock
							trade_goods = fur
						}
					}
				}
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					value = 3
					has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wool
						trade_goods = ivory
						trade_goods = livestock
						trade_goods = fur
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centaur_loyal_population
			duration = -1
		}
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = centaur_ensured_loyalties_prov
				duration = 1825
			}
			every_neighbor_province = { #add modifier to OWNED neighbor provinces
				limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = centaur_ensured_loyalties_prov
					duration = 1825
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Middlemen of the Plains
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = centaur_COT_free_development
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = centaur_COT_capital	
			}
			remove_province_modifier = centaur_COT_capital
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = centaur_COT_capital
					duration = -1
				}
				add_base_production = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Generic Centaur MT
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = centaur_free_temple
			capital_scope = { has_tax_building_trigger = no }
		}
		capital_scope = {
			add_building_construction = {
				building = temple
				cost = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

apply_black_herd_capital_NZOC_effects = {
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = I55 } } } #Black Herd
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = I55_tomb_of_the_unchained
				units_in_province = owner
				owner = {
					OR = {
						is_overall_advancing_magic = yes
						is_advancing_any_project = yes
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { set_variable = { tomb_chained_exp = 0 } }
			while = {
				limit = { units_in_province = owner }
				kill_units = { who = owner amount = 1 }
				owner = { change_variable = { tomb_chained_exp = 0.5 } }
			}
			owner = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_overall_advancing_school = { school = necromancy }
							is_advancing_specific_project = { project = black_herd_project_lichdom }
							is_advancing_specific_project = { project = black_herd_project_1 }
						}
					}
					multiply_variable = {
						which = tomb_chained_exp
						value = 4
					}
				}
				increase_magic_experience = { unmodified_var_amount = tomb_chained_exp }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = I55_home_of_the_greatbound }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = I55_home_of_the_greatbound_sub
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = I55_land_of_the_frostclaimed }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = I55_deposit_divination_half_mod
				duration = 3650 #10 years
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = I55_vanishing_migration } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { culture = owner } }
				change_culture = owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religion = owner } }
				change_religion = owner
			}
			owner = {
				export_to_variable = {
					which = bh_manpower_var
					value = base_manpower
					who = PREV
				}
				divide_variable = {
					which = bh_manpower_var
					value = 2
				}
				round_variable = {
					which = bh_manpower_var
					value = 1
				}
				for_variable_amount = {
					variable = bh_manpower_var
					effect = "
						PREV = {
							add_base_manpower = -1
							add_base_production = 1
						}
					"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

add_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_province_flag = cen_double_nzoc_effects_flag }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = base_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = base_nomadic_zone_of_control
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

add_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_province_flag = cen_double_nzoc_effects_flag }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

add_nomadic_capital_moved_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = { #Black Herd
			$scope$ = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = I55_tomb_of_the_unchained
					has_province_modifier = I55_home_of_the_greatbound
					has_province_modifier = I55_land_of_the_frostclaimed
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = nomadic_capital_just_moved
			duration = 365 #1 year
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = nomadic_capital_just_moved
			duration = 1095 #3 years
		}
	}
}

remove_centaur_nomadism = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control }
			remove_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control_double }
			remove_province_modifier = base_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control }
			remove_province_modifier = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control_double }
			remove_province_modifier = base_noncentaur_nomadic_zone_of_control_double
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = nomadic_capital_just_moved }
			remove_country_modifier = nomadic_capital_just_moved
		}
		clr_country_flag = has_centaur_nomadism_attribute

		if = { #Golden Tremor
			limit = { has_saved_global_event_target = I57_permanent_capital_target }
			set_capital = event_target:I57_permanent_capital_target
			clear_global_event_target = I57_permanent_capital_target
		}
	}
}

golden_highway_cant_construct_tt = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				golden_highway_$section$ = {
					type = all
					country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
				}
			}			
		}
		custom_tooltip = own_all_provinces_in_golden_highway_$section$_tt
	}
}

golden_highway_select_next_province = {
	random_neighbor_province = {
		limit = {
			province_group = golden_highway_$section$
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = golden_highway }
		}
		save_event_target_as = golden_highway_next_province
	}
}

golden_highway_complete_construction = {
	add_permanent_province_modifier = {
		name = golden_highway
		duration = -1
	}
	#Ash Palace tier 3
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					owner = { owns = 625 }
					625 = { has_great_project = { type = ash_palace tier = 3 } }
				}
				AND = {
					# Nansalen also getting Ash Palace tier 3 buff if Akalses has it.
					owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F80 } mission_completed = F80_mission_not_so_far_anymore }
					625 = { 
						owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F33 } }
						has_great_project = {
							type = ash_palace
							tier = 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { 
			name = golden_highway_v2
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
	# Parusahan Saya MT - The Iron Spirit Privilege
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_raj_ministries_the_iron_spirit }
		}
		add_province_modifier = { 
			name = R54_golden_veins
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

increase_legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod = {
	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = has_country_modifier
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod0 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod0 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod1 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod1 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod1 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod2 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod2 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod2 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod3 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod3 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod3 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod4 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod4 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod4 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod5 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod5 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod5 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod6 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod6 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod6 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod7 duration = -1 } }

	}
}

		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod6 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod6 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod5 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod7 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod7 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod6 duration = -1 } }
		legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod8 = { remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod8 add_country_modifier = { name = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod7 duration = -1 } }
	}
}

calc_legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups = {
	remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod0
	remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod1
	remove_country_modifier = legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod2

anb_add_extra_mage_tower_dev = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = unlocked_extra_dev_on_mage_tower }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = built_dev_mage_tower }
		}
		add_base_production = 1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = built_dev_mage_tower
		}
	}
}

anb_remove_extra_mage_tower_dev = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = unlocked_extra_dev_on_mage_tower }
			has_province_flag = built_dev_mage_tower
		}
		add_base_production = -1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = built_dev_mage_tower
		}
	}
}

switch_bayvic_to_bayvek = {
	723 = {
		change_culture = city_goblin
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			Z28 = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = bayvic_to_bayvek_done }
			}
		}
		Z28 = {
			change_primary_culture = city_goblin
			set_country_flag = no_longer_monstrous
			add_accepted_culture = blue_reachman
			override_country_name = BAYVEK
			set_country_flag = bayvic_to_bayvek_done
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			723 = {
				change_province_name = "Bayvek" #avoid double rename tooltip + else the prov name switches back to Bayvic if not owned by a goblin tag
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			Z28 = {
				exists = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = bayvic_to_bayvek_done }
			}
		}
		723 = {
			change_province_name = "Bayvek"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			Z28 = {
				change_primary_culture = city_goblin
				set_country_flag = no_longer_monstrous
				add_accepted_culture = blue_reachman
				override_country_name = BAYVEK
				set_country_flag = bayvic_to_bayvek_done
			}
		}
	}
}

select_highest_dev_province_with_limit = {
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = { $limit$ }
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = highest_dev_province_with_limit$index$ }
			if = {
				limit = { higher_development_than = event_target:highest_dev_province_with_limit$index$ }
				save_event_target_as = highest_dev_province_with_limit$index$
			}
		}
		else = { save_event_target_as = highest_dev_province_with_limit$index$ }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_saved_event_target = highest_dev_province_with_limit$index$ }
		[[effect] event_target:highest_dev_province_with_limit$index$ = { $effect$ } ]
	}
}

select_highest_dev_known_country_with_limit = {
	every_known_country = {
		limit = { $limit$ }
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = highest_dev_known_country_with_limit$index$ }
			if = {
				limit = { total_own_and_non_tributary_subject_development = event_target:highest_dev_known_country_with_limit$index$ }
				save_event_target_as = highest_dev_known_country_with_limit$index$
			}
		}
		else = { save_event_target_as = highest_dev_known_country_with_limit$index$ }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_saved_event_target = highest_dev_known_country_with_limit$index$ }
		[[effect] event_target:highest_dev_known_country_with_limit$index$ = { $effect$ } ]
	}
}

select_highest_dev_province_in_location_with_limit = {
	$location$ = {
		type = all
		limit = { $limit$ }
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = highest_dev_province_in_$location$$index$ }
			if = {
				limit = { higher_development_than = event_target:highest_dev_province_in_$location$$index$ }
				save_event_target_as = highest_dev_province_in_$location$$index$
			}
		}
		else = {
			save_event_target_as = highest_dev_province_in_$location$$index$
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_saved_event_target = highest_dev_province_in_$location$$index$ }
		[[effect]
			event_target:highest_dev_province_in_$location$$index$ = { $effect$ }
		]
	}
}

add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = {
	custom_tooltip = add_$value$_ae_tt
	[[desc] custom_tooltip = $desc$ ]
	hidden_effect = {
		every_known_country = {
			[[limit] limit = { $limit$ } ]
			add_aggressive_expansion = {
				who = PREV
				value = $value$
				[[apply_calc] apply_calc = $apply_calc$ ]
			}
			[[effect] $effect$]
		}
	}
}

#only does base-game modifications rn. do modded ones by surrounding this effect with the set and remove flag. Please note - you need three modifications total (base-game or modded, doesn't matter) in the argument or else the game WILL crash!
create_flagship_with_modifications = {
	owner = {
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_captains_log
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_spare_jolly_roger
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_flag_officers
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_standardized_signal_book
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_mortars
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_improved_crows_nest
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_command_aftercastle
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_trade_route_map
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_mass_load_cannons
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_integrated_marines
		set_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_hull_sheating

		[[captains_log] 			clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_captains_log ]
		[[spare_jolly_roger] 		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_spare_jolly_roger ]
		[[flag_officers]			clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_flag_officers ]
		[[standardized_signal_book]	clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_standardized_signal_book ]
		[[mortars]					clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_mortars ]
		[[improved_crows_nest]		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_improved_crows_nest ]
		[[command_aftercastle]		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_command_aftercastle ]
		[[trade_route_map]			clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_trade_route_map ]
		[[mass_load_cannons]		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_mass_load_cannons ]
		[[integrated_marines]		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_integrated_marines ]
		[[hull_sheating]			clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_hull_sheating ]
	}
	create_flagship = {
		name = "$name$"
		type = $type$
	}
	owner = {
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_captains_log
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_spare_jolly_roger
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_flag_officers
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_standardized_signal_book
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_mortars
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_improved_crows_nest
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_command_aftercastle
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_trade_route_map
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_mass_load_cannons
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_integrated_marines
		clr_country_flag = forbid_flagship_modification_flag_hull_sheating
	}
}

select_highest_opinion_country_with_limit = {
	set_variable = {
		which = highest_opinion_check
		value = 0
	}
	every_known_country = {
		limit = { $limit$ }
		export_to_variable = {
			which = temp_opinion_check
			value = opinion
			with = ROOT
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = temp_opinion_check
				which = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ROOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = temp_opinion_check
						which = highest_opinion_check
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = highest_opinion_check
					which = temp_opinion_check
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = highest_opinion_country_with_limit
		}
		[[effect] event_target:highest_opinion_country_with_limit = { $effect$ }]
	}

}

force_ai_convert = { #Stops the ai from converting back immediately if their RU is too low
	if = {
		limit = { ai = yes }
		force_converted = yes
	}
}

remove_random_development = { #Unlike add_random_development = -1, this won't attempt to remove development at 1
	random_list = {
		1 = {
			trigger = { base_tax = 2 }
			add_base_tax = -1
		}
		1 = {
			trigger = { base_production = 2 }
			add_base_production = -1
		}
		1 = {
			trigger = { base_manpower = 2 }
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
	}
}

define_heir_with_minimum_stats = { #This makes it so if your generated heir is below the amount, the stat will be increased to match
	export_to_variable = {
		variable_name = heir_adm_var
		value = heir_adm
		who = ROOT
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = heir_adm_sub
		value = $adm_amount$ 
	}
	export_to_variable = {
		variable_name = heir_dip_var
		value = heir_dip
		who = ROOT
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = heir_dip_sub
		value = $dip_amount$ 
	}
	export_to_variable = {
		variable_name = heir_mil_var
		value = heir_mil
		who = ROOT
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = heir_mil_sub
		value = $mil_amount$ 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = heir_adm_sub
				which = heir_adm_var
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = heir_adm_sub
			which = heir_adm_var
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = heir_adm_sub
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = heir_adm_sub
				value = -1
			}
			change_heir_adm = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = heir_dip_sub
				which = heir_dip_var
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = heir_dip_sub
			which = heir_dip_var
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = heir_dip_sub
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = heir_dip_sub
				value = -1
			}
			change_heir_dip = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = heir_mil_sub
				which = heir_mil_var
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = heir_mil_sub
			which = heir_mil_var
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = heir_mil_sub
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = heir_mil_sub
				value = -1
			}
			change_heir_mil = 1
		}
	}
}

anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { #The in-engine version is bugged, won't give dip power
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					accepted_culture = $culture$
					primary_culture = $culture$
				}
			}
			add_dip_power = 100
		}
	}
	add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = $culture$ [[dip_reward] dip_reward = $dip_reward$] [[free] free = $free$] }
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					accepted_culture = $culture$
					primary_culture = $culture$
				}
			}
			add_dip_power = 100
		}
	}
	[[dip_reward]
		custom_tooltip = ADD_ACCEPTED_CULTURE_SLOT_LIMITATION_TT #If the Culture is already an Accepted Culture, or if there are not enough Slots, gain 100 Diplomatic Power instead.
	]
}

#Half Elf colony transition
anb_colony_becomes_human = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			culture_group = lencori
		}
		if = {

				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						culture = high_lorentish 
					}
				}
			}
			change_culture = high_lorentish

#Switch to a Human Culture within the same group
anb_changed_ways_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			culture_group = lencori
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				dominant_culture = high_lorentish
			}
			change_primary_culture = high_lorentish
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				dominant_culture = low_lorentish
			}
			change_primary_culture = low_lorentish
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				dominant_culture = derannic
			}

prepare_months_of_tax_income = {
	hidden_effect = {
		export_to_variable = {
			which = current_tax_income
			value = monthly_income
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = tax_income_share
			value = trigger_value:tax_income_percentage
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = current_tax_income
			which = tax_income_share
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = current_tax_income
			value = $months$
		}
		round_variable = {
			which = current_tax_income
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

prepare_months_of_trade_income = {
	hidden_effect = {
		export_to_variable = {
			which = current_trade_income
			value = monthly_income
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = trade_income_share
			value = trigger_value:trade_income_percentage
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = current_trade_income
			which = trade_income_share
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = current_trade_income
			value = $months$
		}
		round_variable = {
			which = current_trade_income
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

add_prepared_months_of_tax_income = {
	hidden_effect = {
		var_effect = { effect = add_treasury var = current_tax_income sign = + }
	}
	custom_tooltip = add_months_of_tax_income_tt
}

remove_prepared_months_of_tax_income = {
	hidden_effect = {
		var_effect = { effect = add_treasury var = current_tax_income sign = - }
	}
	custom_tooltip = remove_months_of_tax_income_tt
}

add_prepared_months_of_trade_income = {
	hidden_effect = {
		var_effect = { effect = add_treasury var = current_trade_income sign = + }
	}
	custom_tooltip = add_months_of_trade_income_tt
}

remove_prepared_months_of_trade_income = {
	hidden_effect = {
		var_effect = { effect = add_treasury var = current_trade_income sign = - }
	}
	custom_tooltip = remove_months_of_trade_income_tt
}

pirate_republic_estate_crownland_setup = {
	change_estate_land_share = {
		estate = estate_adventurers
		share = 40
	}
	change_estate_land_share = {
		estate = estate_mages
		share = 30
	}
}

anb_block_heir_death = { #Blocks heirs from dying, barring events
	[[country] #Is only removable through effects or expiration
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = anb_heir_cannot_die
			duration = $duration$
			hidden = yes
		}
	]
	[[ruler] #Removed through effects or when ruler dies and expiration (Yes, using has_country_modifier works on this )
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = anb_heir_cannot_die
			duration = $duration$
			hidden = yes
		}
	]
}

anb_block_consort_death = {  #Blocks consorts from dying, barring events
	[[country] #Is only removable through effects or expiration
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = anb_consort_cannot_die
			duration = $duration$
			hidden = yes
		}
	]
	[[ruler] #Removed through effects or when ruler dies and expiration (Yes, using has_country_modifier works on this )
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = anb_consort_cannot_die
			duration = $duration$
			hidden = yes
		}
	]
}

anb_allow_heir_death = { #Allows heirs to die again
	remove_country_modifier = anb_heir_cannot_die
}

anb_allow_consort_death = { #Allows consorts to die again (P.S if consort is above 100, they are removed from existence, no notif)
	remove_country_modifier = anb_consort_cannot_die
}

anb_imperial_cultural_union = { #Accept all EoA imperial cultures for free without taking a slot
	custom_tooltip = anb_imperial_cultural_union_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = anbennarian
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}
			# don't do this if they have a cultural union over these cultures anyway
			# since you otherwise gift any empire a couple hundred dip

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = anbenncoster }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = half_elf }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = west_damerian }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = east_damerian }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = pearlsedger }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = crownsman }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = vernman }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = exwesser }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = arbarani }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = esmari }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = arannese }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = uelairey }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = aldresian }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = telgeiran }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = pashainey }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = havoric }

			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = anbenncoster free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = half_elf free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = west_damerian free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = east_damerian free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = pearlsedger free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = crownsman free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = vernman free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = exwesser free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = arbarani free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = esmari free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = arannese free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = uelairey free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = aldresian free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = telgeiran free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = pashainey free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = havoric free = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = halfling
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = imperial_halfling }

			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = imperial_halfling free = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = gnomish
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = imperial_gnome }
			
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = imperial_gnome free = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = gnollish
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = dovesworn_gnoll }
			
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = dovesworn_gnoll free = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = elven
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = moon_elf }
			
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = moon_elf free = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = dwarven
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = silver_dwarf }
			
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = silver_dwarf free = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = alenic
						government_rank = 3
					}
				}
			}

			# So that they become free
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = wexonard }
			anb_remove_accepted_culture = { culture = vertesker }
			
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = wexonard free = yes }
			anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = vertesker free = yes }
		}
	}
}

zaradyrra_invite_scholar = {
	add_adm_power = -25
	clear_religious_scholar_modifiers_effect = yes
	zaradyrra_invite_$scholar$_effect = yes
}
zaradyrra_invite_blade_and_needle_effect = {
    custom_tooltip = zaradyrra_invite_blade_and_needle_scholar_tt
    if = {
        limit = {
            religious_school = {
                group = lizardfolk_religion
                school = humble_zeal_school
            }
        }
        country_event = { id = zaradyrra.11 days = 3650 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            religious_school = {
                group = lizardfolk_religion
                school = soul_song_school
            }
        }
        country_event = { id = zaradyrra.12 days = 3650 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            religious_school = {
                group = lizardfolk_religion
                school = colors_of_life_school
            }
        }
        country_event = { id = zaradyrra.10 days = 3650 }
    }
	custom_tooltip = zaradyrra_deity_tt
    add_country_modifier = { name = blade_and_needle_scholar_modifier duration = 3650 }
}
zaradyrra_invite_great_cycle_effect = {
    custom_tooltip = zaradyrra_invite_great_cycle_scholar_tt

}

    add_country_modifier = { name = colors_of_life_scholar_modifier duration = 3650 }
}
zaradyrra_festivals_of_blood_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ashhana_festivals_of_blood_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = festivals_of_blood_festival_effect_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = festivals_of_blood_modifier
				duration = 3650
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_units_of_type_in_province = {
					amount = 5
					who = ROOT
					unit_type = infantry
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = ashhana_festivals_of_blood_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

give_bladeskeep_monument_worthy_reward = {
    custom_tooltip = bladeskeep_monument_can_use.tt
    hidden_effect = {
        set_country_flag = bladeskeep_monument_is_worthy
        if = {
            limit = { owns = 817 }
            817 = {
                remove_province_modifier = bladeskeep_monument_not_steward
                add_province_modifier = {
                    name = bladeskeep_monument_steward
                    duration = -1
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
gain_yearly_tribute = { #Effect similar to the yearly tribute
	hidden_effect = {
		[[ducats]
			#12.5% of yearly income rounded down
			export_to_variable = {
				which = tributary_monthly_income
				value = trigger_value:monthly_income
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = tributary_monthly_income
				value = 12
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = tributary_monthly_income
				value = 0.125
			}
			round_variable = {
				which = tributary_monthly_income
				value = -1
			}
			overlord = {
				set_variable = {
					which = tributary_monthly_income
					which = PREV
				}
				var_effect = { effect = add_treasury var = tributary_monthly_income sign = + }
			}
		]
		[[manpower]
		#25% of yearly manpower - (Max Manpower * (1 + Manpower Recovery Speed))/10
			export_to_variable = {
				which = tributary_max_manpower
				value = trigger_value:max_manpower
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = tributary_manpower_recovery
				value = modifier:manpower_recovery_speed
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = tributary_manpower_recovery
				value = 1
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = tributary_max_manpower
				which = tributary_manpower_recovery
			}
			divide_variable = {
				which = tributary_max_manpower
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = tributary_max_manpower
				value = 0.25
			}
			overlord = {
				set_variable = {
					which = tributary_max_manpower
					which = PREV
				}
				var_effect_granular = { effect = add_manpower var = tributary_max_manpower sign = + }
			}
		]
		[[mana]
			#Adm/Dip/Mil - Total Development/33 (Max 12 + Monarch Power Tribute) 
			export_to_variable = {
				which = tributary_total_dev
				value = trigger_value:total_development
			}
			divide_variable = {
				which = tributary_total_dev
				value = 33
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = overlord_bonus_tribute_power
				value = modifier:monarch_power_tribute
				who = overlord
			}
			if = { #If the total monarch power is above 12, decrease it
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = tributary_total_dev
						value = 12
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = tributary_total_dev
					value = 12
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = tributary_total_dev
				which = overlord_bonus_tribute_power
			}
			while = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = tributary_total_dev
						value = 1
					}
				}
				overlord = {
					random_list = {
						1 = { add_adm_power = 1 }
						1 = { add_dip_power = 1 }
						1 = { add_mil_power = 1 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = tributary_total_dev
					value = -1
				}
			}
		]
	}
}

#School Variable Change Anzalkatsa Addition
anb_lizardfolk_clash_change_variable_plus = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			6150 = {
				NOT = { is_variable_equal = { which = lizSchoolFightVar value = 3 } }
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = 333rdformed }  
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			6150 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = lizSchoolFightVar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				6150 = { is_variable_equal = { which = lizSchoolFightVar value = 2 } }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school_humiliated
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = fate_sculptors_school_ascended
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school_ascended
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = being_sculptors_school_humiliated
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = fate_ascended_once}
					}
					country_event = { id = AnzalkatsaSchoolFightEvents.19 }	
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				6150 = { is_variable_equal = { which = lizSchoolFightVar value = -1 } }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school_humiliated
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school_ascended
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = fate_sculptors_school
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school_humiliated
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school_ascended
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = being_sculptors_school
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
	}
}

#School Variable Change Anzalkatsa subtraction
anb_lizardfolk_clash_change_variable_minus = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			6150 = {
				NOT = { is_variable_equal = { which = lizSchoolFightVar value = -3 } }
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = 333rdformed }  
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			6150 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = lizSchoolFightVar
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				6150 = { is_variable_equal = { which = lizSchoolFightVar value = -2 } }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school_ascended
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = fate_sculptors_school_humiliated
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school_humiliated
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = being_sculptors_school_ascended
					}
				}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = being_ascended_once}
				}
				country_event = { id = AnzalkatsaSchoolFightEvents.18 }	
			}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				6150 = { is_variable_equal = { which = lizSchoolFightVar value = 1 } }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school_humiliated
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = fate_sculptors_school_ascended
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = fate_sculptors_school
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school_ascended
							}
							religious_school = {
								group = lizardfolk_religion
								school = being_sculptors_school_humiliated
							}
						}
					}
					set_religious_school = {
						group = lizardfolk_religion
						school = being_sculptors_school
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
	}
}

#Port Jaher
ascajar_accepted_culture_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = { 
			365 = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = ascajar
					tier = 3
				}
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = ascajar_culture_mod1
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = ascajar_culture_mod2
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			365 = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = ascajar
					tier = 1
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = ascajar_culture_mod1
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}
ascajar_remove_culture_modifier = {
	remove_province_modifier = ascajar_culture_mod1
	remove_province_modifier = ascajar_culture_mod2
}

	if = {
		limit = {

		add_province_modifier = {
			name = oasis_of_water_dreams_fmk_mod3
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {

jadd_holy_order_reformed = {
	export_to_variable = { which = holyOrderCost value = modifier:establish_order_cost who = ROOT }
	multiply_variable = { which = holyOrderCost value = 50 }
	change_variable = { which = holyOrderCost value = 50 }
	set_variable = { which = adm_order_refund value = 0 }
	set_variable = { which = dip_order_refund value = 0 }
	set_variable = { which = mil_order_refund value = 0 }
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			holy_order = lightbringers_order
		}
		set_province_flag = lightbringers_order_was_here
	}
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			holy_order = jasienes_daughters_order
		}
		set_province_flag = jasienes_daughters_was_here
	}
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			holy_order = militant_jadd_order
		}
		set_province_flag = militant_jadd_order_was_here
	}
	set_country_flag = the_jadd_holy_order_reformed
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = lightbringers_order_was_here
		}
		every_province_in_state = {
			clr_province_flag = lightbringers_order_was_here
		}
		holy_order = lightbringers_order_upgraded
		owner = { change_variable = { which = adm_order_refund which = holyOrderCost } }
	}
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = jasienes_daughters_was_here
		}
		every_province_in_state = {
			clr_province_flag = jasienes_daughters_was_here
		}
		holy_order = jasienes_daughters_order_upgraded
		owner = { change_variable = { which = dip_order_refund which = holyOrderCost } }
	}
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = militant_jadd_order_was_here
		}
		every_province_in_state = {
			clr_province_flag = militant_jadd_order_was_here
		}
		holy_order = militant_jadd_order_upgraded
		owner = { change_variable = { which = mil_order_refund which = holyOrderCost } }
	}
	if = { #just in case establish_order_cost exceeds -100% which would start giving free power
		limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = holyOrderCost value = 0 } } }
		multiply_variable = { which = adm_order_refund value = -1 }
		multiply_variable = { which = dip_order_refund value = -1 }
		multiply_variable = { which = mil_order_refund value = -1 }
		var_effect = { effect = add_adm_power var = adm_order_refund sign = - }
		var_effect = { effect = add_dip_power var = dip_order_refund sign = - }
		var_effect = { effect = add_mil_power var = mil_order_refund sign = - }
	}
	else = {
		var_effect = { effect = add_adm_power var = adm_order_refund sign = + }
		var_effect = { effect = add_dip_power var = dip_order_refund sign = + }
		var_effect = { effect = add_mil_power var = mil_order_refund sign = + }
	}
}

add_glasslord_network = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 10 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_10
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 9 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_9
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 8 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_8
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 7 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_7
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 6 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_6
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 5 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_5
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 4 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_4
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = glasslord_wine_CoTs value = 3 } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = glasslord_network_3
			duration = -1
		}

			duration = -1

			duration = -1

add_yearly_income_capped = {
	hidden_effect = {
		export_to_variable = {
			which = monthly_income
			value = trigger_value:monthly_income
		}
		multiply_variable = { 
			which = monthly_income
			value = 12
		}
		multiply_variable = { #This is yearly
			which = monthly_income
			value = $years$
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = monthly_income
					value = $cap$
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = monthly_income
				value = $cap$
			}
		}
		var_effect = { effect = add_treasury var = monthly_income sign = $sign$ }
	}
}

rinta_seeker_adeen_revolt = {
	S78 = {
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { NOT = { is_subject = yes } } }
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
				who = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { is_subject = yes } }
			hidden_effect = {
				ROOT = {
					overlord = {
						save_event_target_as = rinta_seekers_overlord_for_attack
					}
				}
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
				who = event_target:rinta_seekers_overlord_for_attack
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			capital_scope = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { province_has_current_tech_fort_trigger = yes } }
					add_latest_building = { builder = ROOT fort = yes }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_building = coastal_defence
								has_building = naval_battery
							}
						}
					}
					add_latest_building = { builder = ROOT coastal = yes }
				}
			}
			create_unit_forcelimit_percentage = {
				type = infantry
				special_unit_category = marines
				force_limit_percentage = 1
			}
			create_unit_forcelimit_percentage = {
				type = galley
				force_limit_percentage = 1
			}
			add_years_of_income = 10
			add_yearly_manpower = 10
			add_yearly_sailors = 10
			set_country_flag = rinta_adeen_rise_war
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_saved_event_target = adeeni_target_1 }
		event_target:adeeni_target_1 = {
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = nationalist_rebels
				female = yes
				size = 2
				friend = S78
				separatists_target = S78
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_core = S78
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = adeeni_target_2 }
			event_target:adeeni_target_2 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = nationalist_rebels
					size = 2
					friend = S78
					separatists_target = S78
					win = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_core = S78
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_saved_event_target = adeeni_target_3 }
				event_target:adeeni_target_3 = {
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = nationalist_rebels
						size = 2
						friend = S78
						separatists_target = S78
						win = yes
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						add_core = S78
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# This is a primitive random number generator. Intended for use in places that require RNG without delay.
# Basically, it's the numbers 0 through 4092 but in an unpredictable order.
# On its own, generates an integer between 0 and 4092 "randnum"
# Generates an integer between 1 and $max$ if you use it that way

# It requires some very specific integers to function properly
# Credit for discovering and measuring these integers goes to:
#
# L�Ecuyer, Pierre. (1999). 'Tables of Linear Congruential Generators of Different Sizes and Good Lattice Structure',
# Mathematics of Computation, 68(225), p249-260 [online].
# Available at: https://www.ams.org/journals/mcom/1999-68-225/S0025-5718-99-00996-5/S0025-5718-99-00996-5.pdf
# (Accessed: 17 April 2025)

randnum_effect = {
	REB = {
		multiply_variable = { randnum = 209 }
		modulo_variable = { randnum = 4093 }
		PREV = { set_variable = { which = randnum which = PREV } }
	}

	[[max]
		modulo_variable = { randnum = $max$ }
		change_variable = { randnum = 1 }
	]
	[[max_var]
		modulo_variable = { which = randnum which = $max_var$ }
		change_variable = { randnum = 1 }
	]

	[[case30]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 30 } }	$case30$ } ]
	[[case29]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 29 } }	$case29$ } ]
	[[case28]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 28 } }	$case28$ } ]
	[[case27]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 27 } }	$case27$ } ]
	[[case26]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 26 } }	$case26$ } ]
	[[case25]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 25 } }	$case25$ } ]
	[[case24]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 24 } }	$case24$ } ]
	[[case23]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 23 } }	$case23$ } ]
	[[case22]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 22 } }	$case22$ } ]
	[[case21]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 21 } }	$case21$ } ]
	[[case20]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 20 } }	$case20$ } ]
	[[case19]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 19 } }	$case19$ } ]
	[[case18]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 18 } }	$case18$ } ]
	[[case17]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 17 } }	$case17$ } ]
	[[case16]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 16 } }	$case16$ } ]
	[[case15]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 15 } }	$case15$ } ]
	[[case14]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 14 } }	$case14$ } ]
	[[case13]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 13 } }	$case13$ } ]
	[[case12]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 12 } }	$case12$ } ]
	[[case11]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 11 } }	$case11$ } ]
	[[case10]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 10 } }	$case10$ } ]
	[[case9]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 9 } }	$case9$ } ]
	[[case8]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 8 } }	$case8$ } ]
	[[case7]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 7 } }	$case7$ } ]
	[[case6]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 6 } }	$case6$ } ]
	[[case5]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 5 } }	$case5$ } ]
	[[case4]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 4 } }	$case4$ } ]
	[[case3]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 3 } }	$case3$ } ]
	[[case2]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 2 } }	$case2$ } ]
	[[case1]	if = { limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = randnum value = 1 } }	$case1$ } ]
}

randnum_recalc = {
	REB = {
		multiply_variable = { randnum = 209 }
		modulo_variable = { randnum = 4093 }
		PREV = { set_variable = { which = randnum which = PREV } }
	}

	[[max]
		modulo_variable = { randnum = $max$ }
		change_variable = { randnum = 1 }
	]
}

truncate_variable_3 = { #truncates a variable to 3 sig figs. assumes a range of 1-100
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { $which$ = 10 } }
		divide_variable = { $which$ = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { $which$ = 100 }
	}
	else = {
		divide_variable = { $which$ = 10 }
		multiply_variable = { $which$ = 10 }
	}
}

define_consort_to_general = { #this is basically just for the magic rework

	[[name]
		set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = simple name = "$consort_name$" }
		set_country_flag = has_consort_name
	]
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = has_consort_name } }
		if = { limit = { has_female_consort = yes }
			set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = advisor female = yes scope = THIS }
		}
		else = { set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = advisor scope = THIS } }
	}
	else = { clr_country_flag = has_consort_name }

	define_general = {
		shock = $shock$
		fire = $fire$
		manuever = $manuever$
		siege = $siege$
		name = consort_name
		[[female] female = $female$ ]
		[[trait] trait = $trait$ ]
	}
	clear_saved_name = consort_name
}

convert_female_consort_to_general = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_female_consort = yes }

		[[name]
			set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = simple name = "$consort_name$" }
			set_country_flag = has_consort_name
		]
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = has_consort_name } }
			set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = advisor female = yes scope = THIS }
		}
		else = { clr_country_flag = has_consort_name }

		create_general = {
			tradition = 0
			name = consort_name # WARNING: Broken for any names with more than 2 parts, ie "Marie Sil Calas" becomes "Marie Calas"
			female = yes
		}

		clear_saved_name = consort_name
	}
}

convert_consort_to_general = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_female_consort = no }

		[[name]
			set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = simple name = "$consort_name$" }
			set_country_flag = has_consort_name
		]
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = has_consort_name } }
			set_saved_name = { key = consort_name type = advisor scope = THIS }
		}
		else = { clr_country_flag = has_consort_name }

		create_general = {
			tradition = 0
			name = consort_name # WARNING: Broken for any names with more than 2 parts, ie "Marie Sil Calas" becomes "Marie Calas"
		}
		
		clear_saved_name = consort_name
	}
}

		limit = { stability = 3}
		add_adm_power = 100
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { stability = 2}
		add_stability = 1
		add_adm_power = 50
	}
	else = {
		add_stability = 2
	}
}

beikling_red_citadel_province_change_effect = {
	if = { #Remove Effects
		limit = { province_id = 4844 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				4844 = {
					has_great_project = {
						type = the_red_citadel
						tier = 1
					}
					can_use_red_citadel_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					4844 = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = the_red_citadel
							tier = 3
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_3
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = the_red_citadel_extra_dev 
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					4844 = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = the_red_citadel
							tier = 2
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_2
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_1
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { #Remove Extrad Dev and Dev Cost
			every_owned_province  = {
				remove_province_modifier = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_1
				remove_province_modifier = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_2
				remove_province_modifier = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = the_red_citadel_extra_dev }
				clr_country_flag = the_red_citadel_extra_dev
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { # Add Effects
		limit = {
			owner = { owns = 4844 }
			4844 = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = the_red_citadel
					tier = 1
				}
				can_use_red_citadel_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		beikling_update_better_forging_effect = yes #Better forging modifier
		if = {
			limit = {
				province_group = beikling_homeland_provinces
			}
			#Extra dev from the monument
			if =  {
				limit = {
					4844 = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = the_red_citadel
							tier = 3
						}
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_3
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if =  {
				limit = {
					4844 = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = the_red_citadel
							tier = 2
						}
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = beikling_homeland_extra_dev_1
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			
			# Iron - Copper Bonus
			if = {
				limit = {
					4974 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = the_masterforge_unlit } }
					owner = { owns = 4974 }
					NOT = { province_id = 4974 }
					OR = {
						trade_goods = iron
						trade_goods = copper
					}
				}
				if = { # Metalurgic Revival
					limit = { 4974 = { has_province_modifier = the_masterforge } }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = metalurgic_revival
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else_if = { # Pinacle of Metalurgy
					limit = { 4974 = { has_province_modifier = the_masterforge_upgrade } }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = pinnacle_of_metallurgy
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Northern Bastion
			limit = {
				5415 = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = legends_of_the_northern_vanguard } }
				owner = { owns = 5415 }
				OR = {
					area = yunghuun_area
					area = choogiaza_area
					area = kheizavho_area
				}
				NOT = { province_id = 5415 }
			}
			if = { #Under the Bastions Watch
				limit = { 5415 = { has_province_modifier = the_northern_bastion } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = under_the_bastions_watch
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Under the Bastions Shadow
				limit = { 5415 = { has_province_modifier = the_northern_bastion_upgrade } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = under_the_bastions_shadow
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Restore Ruins
	if = { #The Masterforge
		limit = {
			province_id = 4974
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = the_masterforge_unlit }
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = the_masterforge_unlit
			duration = -1
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province  = {
				remove_province_modifier = beikling_better_forging
				remove_province_modifier = metalurgic_revival
				remove_province_modifier = pinnacle_of_metallurgy
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { #The Dark Temple
		limit = {
			province_id = 4952
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = the_empty_visage }
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = the_empty_visage
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = { #The Yan Toll
		limit = { 
			province_id = 4842 
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = an_abandoned_toll }
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = an_abandoned_toll
			duration = -1
		}
		4844 = { #Bianfang Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS
			}
		}
		4925 = { #Tianlou Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS
			}
		}
		4879 = { #Feiten Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS
			}
		}
		4859 = { #Yanzhong Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS
			}		
		}
		4559 = { #Xianjie Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS
			}		
		}
		4633 = { #Shamakhad Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS
			}		
		}
		4500 = { #Kharunyana Node
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = FROM
				key = STRANGLING_HALESS	
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { #The Northern Bastion
		limit = { 
			province_id = 5415
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = legends_of_the_northern_vanguard }
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = legends_of_the_northern_vanguard
			duration = -1
		}
		yunghuun_area = { 
			remove_province_modifier = under_the_bastions_watch
			remove_province_modifier = under_the_bastions_shadow 
		}
		choogiaza_area = { 
			remove_province_modifier = under_the_bastions_watch 
			remove_province_modifier = under_the_bastions_shadow 
		}
		kheizavho_area = { 
			remove_province_modifier = under_the_bastions_watch 
			remove_province_modifier = under_the_bastions_shadow 
		}
	}
}

#type = army/navy
#leader = general/conquistador/admiral/explorer
create_leader_scaling_with_tradition_vic_league_1 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			$type$_tradition = 90
		}
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 100
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			$type$_tradition = 80
		}
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 90
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			$type$_tradition = 70
		}
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 80
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			$type$_tradition = 60
		}
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 70
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			$type$_tradition = 50
		}
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 60
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			$type$_tradition = 40
		}
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 50
		}
	}
	else = {
		create_$leader$ = {
			tradition = 40
		}
	}
	custom_tooltip = create_leader_scaling_with_tradition_tt
}

create_vic_league_member = { #'overlord' can only be ROOT or a specific TAG (PREV won't work). 'subject' can be ROOT, PREV (if the effect is used inside the future subject scope) or a specific TAG
	$overlord$ = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = vic_league_member
			subject = $subject$
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government_attribute = expand_the_league_2_attribute }
			$subject$ = {
				capital_scope = {
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = $overlord$
						duration = -1
						power = 25
						key = vic_commonwealth_trade_bonus
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = vic_league_expand_the_league_upgrade_tt
		}
	}
}

tag_or_overlord_add_spy_network_from = { #use this inside the same country scope you'd use add_spy_network_from. 
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		add_spy_network_from = {
			who = $who$
			value = $value$
		}
	}
	else = {
		overlord = {
			add_spy_network_from = {
				who = $who$
				value = $value$
			}
		}
	}
}

#Building Mover Script for Eordand Event #27
copy_building_to_target_province = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_building = $building$
            [[gold]$target$ = { NOT = { trade_goods = gold } }]
        }
        $target$ = {
            add_building = $building$
        }
    }
}

copy_building_category_to_target_province = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_$category1$_building_trigger = yes
            [[gold]$target$ = { NOT = { trade_goods = gold } }]
        }
        $target$ = {
            add_latest_building = { builder = ROOT $category2$ = yes }
        }
    }
}

sareyand_expand_exorcist_priesthood_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = sareyand_allow_monks }
			superregion = bulwar_superregion
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = rightful_exorcist_priesthood_territory
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { area_for_scope_province = { has_province_modifier = sareyand_exorcist_priest_base } }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = sareyand_exorcist_priest_base
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

sareyand_remove_exorcist_priesthood_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = sareyand_allow_monks }
			superregion = bulwar_superregion
		}
		remove_province_modifier = sareyand_exorcist_priest_base
		remove_province_modifier = rightful_exorcist_priesthood_territory
	}
}

lencori_behemoth_update_all_shipyards = {
	hidden_effect = {
		# also pre-calculate how much production of naval supplies is needed to build another
		# counts down negative numbers to work around the quirky way this system uses calc_true_if
		set_variable = {
			which = lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies
			value = -5
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_port = yes
				has_lencori_behemoth_shipyard = yes
			}
			# put the appropriate province modifier according to your upgrades/privileges
			lencori_behemoth_update_shipyard_modifier = { count = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = improved_behemoth_construction }
			divide_variable = {
				which = lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies
				value = 3
			}
		}
		# prepare a value for the tooltip
		export_lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies_value_for_tt = yes
	}
}

export_lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies_value_for_tt = { 
	set_variable = {
		which = lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies_value_for_tt
		which = lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		which = lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies_value_for_tt
		value = -1
	}
}

lencori_behemoth_add_shipyard_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = improved_behemoth_construction } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_push_for_impressment } } }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = lencori_behemoth_shipyard
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = lencori_behemoth_shipyard_impress
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_push_for_impressment } } }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = lencori_behemoth_shipyard_improved
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = lencori_behemoth_shipyard_impress_improved
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

lencori_behemoth_update_shipyard_modifier = {
	remove_province_modifier = lencori_behemoth_shipyard
	remove_province_modifier = lencori_behemoth_shipyard_impress
	remove_province_modifier = lencori_behemoth_shipyard_improved
	remove_province_modifier = lencori_behemoth_shipyard_impress_improved
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
							value = 5
							has_lencori_behemoth_shipyard = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_control_over_behemoth_shipyards
						NOT = {
							num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
								value = 10
								has_lencori_behemoth_shipyard = yes
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = improved_behemoth_construction
						NOT = {
							num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
								value = 15
								has_lencori_behemoth_shipyard = yes
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = improved_behemoth_construction
						has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_control_over_behemoth_shipyards
						NOT = {
							num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
								value = 20
								has_lencori_behemoth_shipyard = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		[[count] owner = { change_variable = { lencori_behemoth_required_naval_supplies = -5 } }]
		lencori_behemoth_add_shipyard_modifier = yes
	}
}
	
create_general_with_current_tradition = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { army_tradition = 20 }
		}
		create_general = {
			tradition = 20
			[[add_fire] add_fire = $add_fire$ ]
			[[add_shock] add_shock = $add_shock$ ]
			[[add_manuever] add_manuever = $add_manuever$ ]
			[[add_siege] add_siege = $add_siege$ ]
			[[name] name = $name$ ]
			[[culture] culture = $culture$ ]
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			army_tradition = 20
			NOT = { army_tradition = 40 }
		}
		create_general = {
			tradition = 40
			[[add_fire] add_fire = $add_fire$ ]
			[[add_shock] add_shock = $add_shock$ ]
			[[add_manuever] add_manuever = $add_manuever$ ]
			[[add_siege] add_siege = $add_siege$ ]
			[[name] name = $name$ ]
			[[culture] culture = $culture$ ]
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			army_tradition = 40
			NOT = { army_tradition = 60 }
		}
		create_general = {
			tradition = 60
			[[add_fire] add_fire = $add_fire$ ]
			[[add_shock] add_shock = $add_shock$ ]
			[[add_manuever] add_manuever = $add_manuever$ ]
			[[add_siege] add_siege = $add_siege$ ]
			[[name] name = $name$ ]
			[[culture] culture = $culture$ ]
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			army_tradition = 60
			NOT = { army_tradition = 80 }
		}
		create_general = {
			tradition = 80
			[[add_fire] add_fire = $add_fire$ ]
			[[add_shock] add_shock = $add_shock$ ]
			[[add_manuever] add_manuever = $add_manuever$ ]
			[[add_siege] add_siege = $add_siege$ ]
			[[name] name = $name$ ]
			[[culture] culture = $culture$ ]
		}
	}
	else = {
		create_general = {
			tradition = 100
			[[add_fire] add_fire = $add_fire$ ]
			[[add_shock] add_shock = $add_shock$ ]
			[[add_manuever] add_manuever = $add_manuever$ ]
			[[add_siege] add_siege = $add_siege$ ]
			[[name] name = $name$ ]
			[[culture] culture = $culture$ ]
		}
	}
}

    random_owned_province = {
        limit = {
            is_state_core = PREV
        }
            add_$devtype$ = 1
	}
    random_owned_province = {
        limit = {
            is_state_core = PREV
        }
            add_$devtype$ = 1
    }
    random_owned_province = {
        limit = {
            is_state_core = PREV
        }
            add_$devtype$ = 1
    }
    add_country_modifier = {
        name = $modifier$
        duration = -1
    }
}

ael_cannor_interactions_effect = {
    add_adm_power = -25
    add_adm_power = -25
    add_mil_power = -25
    add_treasury = -50
    $tag$ = {
        if = {
            limit = { total_development = 600 }
        	define_advisor = { 
            	type = $advisor$
            	skill = 5
            	cost_multiplier = 0.25
        	}
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { total_development = 450 }
            define_advisor = { 
            	type = $advisor$
            	skill = 4
            	cost_multiplier = 0.25
        	}
        }
		else_if = {
            limit = { total_development = 300 }
        	define_advisor = { 
            	type = $advisor$
            	skill = 3
            	cost_multiplier = 0.25
        	}
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { total_development = 150 }
            define_advisor = { 
            	type = $advisor$
            	skill = 2
            	cost_multiplier = 0.25
        	}
        }
		else = {
            define_advisor = { 
            	type = $advisor$
            	skill = 1
            	cost_multiplier = 0.25
        	}
        }
	}
}
