# binary tree (min:0 max:15)
export_number_of_estate_privs_to_var = {
	if = { # x >= 8
		limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 8 } }
		if = { # x >= 12
			limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 12 } }
			if = { # x >= 14
				limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 14 } }
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 15 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 15 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 14 }
				}
			}
			else = { # 12 <= x < 14
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 13 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 13 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 12 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # 8 <= x < 12
			if = { # 10 <= x < 12
				limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 10 } }
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 11 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 11 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 10 }
				}
			}
			else = { # 8 <= x < 10
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 9 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 9 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # x < 8
		if = { # 4 <= x < 8
			limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 4 } }
			if = { # 6 <= x < 8
				limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 6 } }
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 7 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 7 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 6 }
				}
			}
			else = { # 4 <= x < 6
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 5 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 5 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # x < 4
			if = { # 2 <= x < 4
				limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 2 } }
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 3 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 3 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = { # x < 2
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_estate_privileges = { estate = $estate$ value = 1 } }
					set_variable = { $var$ = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { $var$ = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

tsukqiao_calc_might_and_right_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = tsukqiao_throne_of_lies_reform }
		#The Good Modifiers 81-100 Legitimacy
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_good_1
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_good_2
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_good_3
		#The Least Bad Modifiers 61-80 Legitimacy
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_least_bad_1
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_least_bad_2
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_least_bad_3
		#The Quite Bad Modifiers 31-60 Legitimacy
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_quite_bad_1
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_quite_bad_2
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_quite_bad_3
		#The Worst Modifiers 0-30 Legitimacy
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_worst_1
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_worst_2
		remove_country_modifier = tsukqiao_might_and_right_worst_3
		#Now calculate how much legitimacy do we have
		if = { #The Worst Modifiers 0-30 Legitimacy
			limit = { NOT = { legitimacy = 31 } }
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_2 } #End by checking the level the system is at, starts at 1 and gets upgrade 2 times
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_worst_3 duration = -1 }
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_worst_2 duration = -1 }
			}
			else = { add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_worst_1 duration = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = { #The Quite Bad Modifiers 31-60 Legitimacy
			limit = { NOT = { legitimacy = 61 } }
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_quite_bad_3 duration = -1 }
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_quite_bad_2 duration = -1 }
			}
			else = { add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_quite_bad_1 duration = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = { #The Least Bad Modifiers 61-80 Legitimacy
			limit = { NOT = { legitimacy = 81 } }
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_least_bad_3 duration = -1 }
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_least_bad_2 duration = -1 }
			}
			else = { add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_least_bad_1 duration = -1 } }
		}
		else = { #The Good Modifiers 81-100 Legitimacy
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_good_3 duration = -1 }
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_good_2 duration = -1 }
			}
			else = { add_country_modifier = { name = tsukqiao_might_and_right_good_1 duration = -1 } }
		}
	}
}

			name = tsukqiao_mask_of_might_3

		}

		add_or_extend_ruler_modifier = {

		}
	}
	else = {

			name = tsukqiao_mask_of_might_1
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

B43_corvuria_crusade_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { A59 = { exists = no } }
		create_vassal = A59 #Corvuria
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { A59 = { ai = yes } }
		A59 = { #Corvuria
			custom_tooltip = B43_remove_vampires.tt
			clr_country_flag = has_vampires_estate
			clr_country_flag = is_just_evil
			tooltip = {
				kill_ruler = yes
				kill_heir = { }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { ruler_is_lich = yes }
					kill_a_lich_effect = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = ruled_by_vampire }
					remove_vampire_immortality = yes
				}
				else = { kill_ruler = yes }
				kill_heir = { }
			}
			hidden_effect = { 
				if = { limit = { B14 = { exists = yes is_subject_of = ROOT } } B14 = { exile_ruler_as = { name = B43_raven_ruler } } ROOT = { inherit = B14 } set_ruler = B43_raven_ruler  }
				else_if = { limit = { B48 = { exists = yes is_subject_of = ROOT } } B48 = { exile_ruler_as = { name = B43_raven_ruler } } ROOT = { inherit = B48 } set_ruler = B43_raven_ruler }
				else = {
					define_ruler = {
						dynasty = "Of Ravenmarch"
						culture = ravenmarcher
					}
				}
				remove_opinion =  {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = declared_war_on_us
				}
			}
			force_remove_rival = ROOT
			add_historical_friend = ROOT
			ROOT = { add_historical_friend = A59 }
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = B43_freed_the_raven
			}
			ROOT = { 
				force_remove_rival = A59 
				add_historical_friend = A59
				add_opinion = {
					who = A59
					modifier = B43_freed_the_raven
				}
			}
		}
		A77 = { #Orda Aldresia
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = B43_freed_the_raven
			}
		}
		add_opinion = {
			who = A77
			modifier = B43_freed_the_raven
		}
	}
}

form_adenica_scripted_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = adventurer_reform }
		set_country_flag = adventurer_derived_government
	}
	change_tag = B58
	set_country_flag = feudal_escann_kingdom
	set_country_flag = no_formable_culture_shift
	if = {
		limit = { OR = { has_reform = adventurer_reform has_country_flag = adventurer_derived_government } }
		adventurer_legacy_effect = yes
		country_event = { id = marcher.1 days = 1 }
		#country_event = { id = adventurer.2 days = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
			change_government = monarchy
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = { restore_country_name = yes }
	774 = {
		move_capital_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = human_administration
		}
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_adenner_culture_provinces
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						culture_is_human = yes
					}
				}
				change_culture = adenner
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ruler_culture = ROOT fast_ruler_is_human = yes }
		set_ruler_culture = adenner
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_heir = yes heir_culture = ROOT fast_heir_is_human = yes }
		set_heir_culture = adenner
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_consort = yes consort_culture = ROOT fast_consort_is_human = yes }
		set_consort_culture = adenner
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = human_administration
		}
		change_primary_culture = adenner
		
	}
	remove_non_electors_emperors_from_empire_effect = yes
	increase_government_rank_scripted_effect = { rank = 2 }
	#Claims
	rohibon_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	adenica_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	taran_plains_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	balmire_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	falsemire_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	verteben_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	valefort_area = { add_permanent_claim = B58 }
	add_prestige = 50
	add_country_modifier = {
		name = "centralization_modifier"
		duration = 7300
	}
	set_country_flag = formed_adenica_flag
	clr_country_flag = knightly_order_adventurer
	#country_event = { id = adventurer.2 days = 10 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_custom_ideas = no }
		country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
	}
	swap_non_generic_missions = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = {
			which = adenicaChivalryMissionsCompleted
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = adenicaReligiousWarsWon
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = adenicaWarsWon
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = adenicaOrcWarsWon
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

destroy_shirgrii_effect = {
	remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_shirgrii_shinukhorchi
	remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_shirgrii_chumijemoya
	remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_shirgrii_ajgriijarul
	remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_shirgrii_kabiurgarko
	remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_shirgrii_ruined_khelorvalshi
	remove_province_modifier = azjakuma_shirgrii_khelorvalshi
}

clear_conq_personalities = {
	remove_ruler_personality_effect = { personality = great_conqueror }
	remove_ruler_personality_effect = { personality = mythical_conqueror }
	remove_country_modifier = great_conqueror_modifier
	remove_country_modifier = mythical_conqueror_modifier
}

create_mythical_conqueror = {
	clear_conq_personalities = yes
	force_add_ruler_personality = { personality = mythical_conqueror_personality }
	add_ruler_modifier = {
		name = mythical_conqueror_modifier
		duration = -1
	}
	set_ai_personality = {
		personality = ai_militarist
		locked = yes
	}
	add_stability = 3
	change_dip = 3
	change_adm = 3
	change_mil = 3
	
	# Back-end
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_conqueror_flag
			}
		}
		REB = { change_variable = { nbGC = 1 } }
	}
	set_country_flag = great_conqueror_flag
}

create_great_conqueror = {
	clear_conq_personalities = yes
	force_add_ruler_personality = { personality = great_conqueror_personality }
	add_ruler_modifier = {
		name = great_conqueror_modifier
		duration = -1
	}
	set_ai_personality = {
		personality = ai_militarist
		locked = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			centaur_can_become_vc = yes
		}
		country_event = { id = great_conqueror.5 days = 1825 }									#Turns you into a centaur variant conqueror
		capital_scope = { add_province_modifier = { name = seat_of_centaur_gc duration = -1 } }
	}
	add_stability = 1
	change_dip = 1
	change_adm = 1
	change_mil = 1
	
	# Back-end
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_conqueror_flag
			}
		}
		REB = { change_variable = { nbGC = 1 } }
	}
	set_country_flag = great_conqueror_flag
}

estate_action_CONTRACT_OUT_TO_ESTATES_PLANETOUCHED = {
	auto_complete_estate_agenda = {
		estate = all
	}
	add_estate_loyalty = {
		estate = estate_planetouched
		loyalty = -10
	}
	add_years_of_income = 0.25
}

#Star Rider
I69_religious_action_murdering = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = I69_tributes_of_the_sects }
		every_known_country = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				religious_school = {
					group = centaur_religion
					school = $school$
				}
			}
			reverse_add_casus_belli = {
				type = cb_force_tributary_mission
				target = ROOT
				months = 240
			}
		}
	}	
}

I69_consensus_annexation = {
	if = { #If Variable is at 3, inherit the subject
		limit = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = I69_$school$_answer
				value = 3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					religious_school = {
						group = centaur_religion
						school = $school$_school
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					inherit = PREV			
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = I69_$school$_answer
					value = 4
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = I69_$school$_answer_4
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = I69_$school$_answer_3
		}
	}
	else_if = { #If Variable is at 2, inherit the subject at the cost of 5 dip points per dev
		limit = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = I69_$school$_answer
				value = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					religious_school = {
						group = centaur_religion
						school = $school$_school
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					export_to_variable = {
						which = I69_annexation_variable
						value = total_development
						who = PREV 
					}
					multiply_variable = {
						which = I69_annexation_variable
						value = 5
					}
					var_effect = { effect = add_dip_power var = I69_annexation_variable sign = - }
					inherit = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = I69_$school$_answer_2
	}
	else_if = { #If Variable is at one, reduce liberty desire of the subject
		limit = { 
			check_variable = {
				which = I69_$school$_answer
				value = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					religious_school = {
						group = centaur_religion
						school = $school$_school
					}
				}
				add_liberty_desire = -25
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = I69_$school$_answer_1
	}
	else = { #Else, nothing
		custom_tooltip = I69_$school$_answer_0
	}
}

		}
	}

form_rezankand_effect = {
	change_tag = H67 #Rezankand
	primary_and_ruler_culture_change = { race = elven new_culture = dawn_elf }

		add_accepted_culture = sun_elf
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				culture = sun_elf
			}
			change_culture = dawn_elf
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					employed_advisor = {
						name = "Karodir I Varamzuir"
						skill = 3
						type = court_mage
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { #Get Karodir
				id = flavor_rezankand.12
				days = 90 #3 Months
			}
		}
	}
}

#Bonecarver
second_chaining_effect = {
	random_war_enemy_country = {
		limit = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = scorched_earth
					devastation = 90
				}
				continent = europe
			} 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = B27_wrecked_flag }
			has_reform = adventurer_reform
		}
		add_treasury = -100
		add_manpower = -5
		add_devotion = -25
		add_adm_power = -100
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = forced_to_end_orcish_purge 
			duration = 3650 # Years, same as all other treaties
		}
		generic_end_purge = { race = orcish }
		hidden_effect ={ 
			country_event = { id = race_setup_events.9 } # Update opinion
		}
		largest_increase_of_orcish_tolerance_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = B27_wrecked_flag
		ROOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				add_base_production = 1
				add_base_manpower = 1
				add_base_tax = 1
				}
		}
	}
}
reduce_anguish_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish
		}
		custom_tooltip = reduce_anguish_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 0
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = anguish_level
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				add_church_power = 100
			}
			else = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = anguish_level
					value = 1
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_1
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_2
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_3
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_4
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_12
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_22
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_32
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish_2
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_32
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_3
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish_2
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_22
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_2
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish_2
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_12
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_1
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
increase_anguish_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish
		}
		custom_tooltip = increase_anguish_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 2
					}
					has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish_2
				}
				add_legitimacy = -10
				add_devotion = -10
				add_republican_tradition = -3
				add_horde_unity = -10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 3
					}
				}
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				change_variable = {
					which = anguish_level
					value = 1
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_1
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_2
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_3
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_4
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_12
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_22
			remove_country_modifier =  B27_anguish_32
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 3
					}
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = B27_anguish_4
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish_2
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_32
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_3
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = anguish_level
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = B27_enable_anguish_2
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_22
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = B27_anguish_2
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
B27_pay_stuff = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = B27_roar_gd
			any_known_country = {
				 is_or_was_tag = { tag = B27 }
			}
		}
		add_manpower = -2.5
		add_church_power = -10
		random_known_country = {
		limit = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = B27 }
			}
			add_manpower = 2.5
			add_church_power = 10
		}
	}
}

innovativeness_per_type_advisor_level_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = innovativeness_per_$type$_advisor_level_effect_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		if = { limit = { has_$type$_advisor_5 = yes } change_innovativeness = 5 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_$type$_advisor_4 = yes } change_innovativeness = 4 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_$type$_advisor_3 = yes } change_innovativeness = 3 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_$type$_advisor_2 = yes } change_innovativeness = 2 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_$type$_advisor = yes } change_innovativeness = 1 }
	}
}

add_years_of_separatism_in_owned_provinces = { #Goes from 1-10, accepts - values
	custom_tooltip = add_$years$_of_separatism_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_province = {
			add_nationalism = $years$
		}
	}
}
